About Medical Care in Hillsborough County

Hillsborough County, Florida is home to 4980 verified medical professionals spanning 33 specialties. The county's healthcare landscape includes specialists in Internal Medicine, Family Medicine, Emergency Medicine, Pediatrics, Anesthesiology, ensuring residents have access to comprehensive medical care.

With doctors practicing in 140 cities across the county, including TAMPA, BRANDON, TEMPLE TERRACE, patients can find quality healthcare close to home. 1505 doctors are also willing to travel, providing additional flexibility for patients with mobility challenges or those in underserved areas.

All doctors listed on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, ensuring accurate credentials and practice information. Our directory helps patients make informed decisions when choosing a healthcare provider in Hillsborough County.

Frequently Asked Questions

How many doctors are in Hillsborough County, Florida?
EliteMD lists 4980 verified medical professionals across 33 specialties in Hillsborough County, Florida. This includes specialists in Internal Medicine, Family Medicine, Emergency Medicine, and more.
What are the top medical specialties in Hillsborough County?
The most represented specialties in Hillsborough County are Internal Medicine (628 doctors), Family Medicine (456 doctors), Emergency Medicine (310 doctors), Pediatrics (267 doctors), Anesthesiology (262 doctors).
Which cities in Hillsborough County have the most doctors?
The cities with the most doctors in Hillsborough County are TAMPA (2819), BRANDON (453), TEMPLE TERRACE (267), RIVERVIEW (177), LUTZ (172).
How are doctors in Hillsborough County verified?
All doctors on EliteMD are verified through the National Provider Identifier (NPI) Registry, a federal database maintained by the Centers for Medicare & Medicaid Services. Each doctor's credentials, specialty, and practice location are confirmed through official records.
Can I find a specialist who will travel to Hillsborough County?
Yes, many specialists on EliteMD are available to travel. Use the "Will Travel" filter on the search page to find doctors willing to come to Hillsborough County for consultations and procedures.
